SimSun;\">翻阅上线的主机资料，找到了云平台密码，但并未发现目标系统。重新整理上线的主机，终于在一台运维的机器上找到了网闸的配置文档。</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 14:45:36","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 14:45:36","title":"FasterXML Jackson-databind 多个远程代码执行漏洞","link":"https://www.secpulse.com/?p=139865","description":"<h1>一、漏洞分析</h1>\n<h2>1 FasterXML Jackson组件介绍</h2>\n<p>FasterXML Jackson是美国FasterXML公司的一款适用于Java的数据处理工具。Jackson-databind是其中的一个具有数据绑定功能的组件。Jackson-databind可以将Java对象转换成json对象，同样也可以将json转换成Java对象。</p>\n<h2>2 漏洞描述</h2>\n<p>近期，Jackson官方发布了几个远程代码执行漏洞信息，问题编号分别是：#2798,#2814(CVE-2020-24616),#2826,#2827。</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2798</p>\n<p>利用类：com.pastdev.httpcomponents.configuration.JndiConfiguration</p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2814（CVE-2020-24616）</p>\n<p>利用类：br.com.anteros.dbcp.AnterosDBCPDataSource</p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2826</p>\n<p>利用类：com.nqadmin.rowset.JdbcRowSetImpl</p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2827</p>\n<p>利用类：org.arrah.framework.rdbms.UpdatableJdbcRowsetImpl</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>这些漏洞都是通过JNDI注入导致远程代码执行，由于Jackson-databind 2.9.10.5及之前的版本里缺少了部分JNDI黑名单类，攻击者可以利用上述缺陷，绕过限制，实现JNDI注入，最终在受害主机上执行任意代码。&#160;</p>\n<h2>3&#160;漏洞复现</h2>\n<p>搭建Jackson-databind 环境，复现漏洞，效果如下图：</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2798</p>\n<p>&#160;<img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片128.png\" title=\"图片128.png\" alt=\"图片1.png\"/></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片216-1024x394.png\" title=\"图片216-1024x394.png\" alt=\"图片2.png\"/></p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2814</p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片317.png\" title=\"图片317.png\" alt=\"图片3.png\"/></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片413-1024x384.png\" title=\"图片413-1024x384.png\" alt=\"图片4.png\"/></p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2826</p>\n<p>&#160;<img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片513.png\" title=\"图片513.png\" alt=\"图片5.png\"/></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片617-1024x414.png\" title=\"图片617-1024x414.png\" alt=\"图片6.png\"/></p>\n<p>Jackson Databind#2827</p>\n<p>&#160;<img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片717.png\" title=\"图片717.png\" alt=\"图片7.png\"/></p>\n<p><img src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片816-1024x358.png\" title=\"图片816-1024x358.png\" alt=\"图片8.png\"/></p>\n<h1>二、影响范围</h1>\n<p><a>目前受影响的</a>Jackson-databind版本：</p>\n<p>Jackson-databind &#60;=&#160;2.9.10.5</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<h1>三、修复建议</h1>\n<p>官方发布的最新版本已修复上述漏洞，请受影响的用户下载最新版本即可防御此漏洞利用攻击。</p>\n<p>下载链接：https://github.com/FasterXML/jackson-databind/releases</p>\n<p><br/></p>\n<h1>四、时间轴</h1>\n<p>2020/8/26&#160;&#160;深信服安全团队监测到FasterXML Jackson-databind 远程代码执行漏洞信息。 &#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</p>\n<p>2020/8/27&#160;&#160;深信服千里目安全实验室成功复现上述漏洞并发布漏洞分析文章。</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<h1>五、参考链接</h1>\n<p><a href=\"https://github.com/FasterXML/jackson-databind/issues/2827\">https://github.com/FasterXML/jackson-databind/issues/2827</a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://github.com/FasterXML/jackson-databind/issues/2814\">https://github.com/FasterXML/jackson-databind/issues/2814</a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://github.com/FasterXML/jackson-databind/issues/2798\">https://github.com/FasterXML/jackson-databind/issues/2798</a></p>\n<p><br/></p>\n","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Fri, 28 Aug 2020 03:13:35 +0000","feedId":5124,"bgimg":"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片128.png","linkMd5":"052de181a86e84e997360b1b8f06ca58","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn52@2020_1/2020/08/31/06-45-39-950_85a3c657d6a9970d.webp","destWidth":981,"destHeight":624,"sourceBytes":136244,"destBytes":28900,"author":"深信服千里目安全实验室","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片128.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn52@2020_1/2020/08/31/06-45-39-950_85a3c657d6a9970d.webp","https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片216-1024x394.png":null,"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片317.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn26@2020_1/2020/08/31/06-45-52-530_e4a6fdc6ecf40927.webp","https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片413-1024x384.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn71@2020_1/2020/08/31/06-45-53-607_d2c27dbe074caccd.webp","https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片513.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn8@2020_6/2020/08/31/06-45-49-200_91ef28049b9272f9.webp","https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片617-1024x414.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn63@2020_6/2020/08/31/06-45-49-305_5eb5d8133c2fb53f.webp","https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片717.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn4@2020_4/2020/08/31/06-45-54-496_6ed26bfc779f19cb.webp","https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/图片816-1024x358.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn5@2020_3/2020/08/31/06-45-47-192_95b1afe962362dec.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598856336298},{"createdTime":"2020-08-31 14:45:36","updatedTime":"2020-08-31 14:45:36","title":"「Burpsuite练兵场」SQL注入及相关实验（一）","link":"https://www.secpulse.com/?p=139667","description":"<p>说到SQL注入漏洞，各位小伙伴一定是耳熟能详，作为一种常见的高危漏洞，其对于应用程序的损害是非常严重的。因此这也是一个在渗透测试的过程中具有高优先级的验证目标，所以将与之相关的实验进行优先讲述。</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center\"><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image407.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image407.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image407.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center\"><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image408.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image408.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image408.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">SQL注入原理：</p>\n<p>SQL注入的原理其实并不难理解，Web应用程序后台获取用户输入并将其拼接到SQL查询语句中进行执行，而这里的用户输入就是我们可以构造恶意payload的地方，通过一些技巧使得查询语句按照我们所希望的方式执行即可完成一次成功的SQL注入。正如大多数的Web漏洞一样，究其漏洞本质就是未验证用户输入，没有实现输入数据与程序执行语句的分离。</p>\n<p>但是由于存在不同的数据库（如常见的Oracle、SQL Server、Mysql等）所导致的具有微小差异性的SQL语句实现，以及我们无法直接观察到后台的查询逻辑，导致我们在实际的SQL注入漏洞搜寻过程当中往往也要花费不小的精力，同时也非常考察我们对于SQL语句的掌握程度。</p>\n<p>话不多说，下面直接进入相关实验及原理的介绍：</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">实验内容</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">注意事项：</span></p>\n<p>1、实验仅对SQL注入原理进行简单阐述，读者需要有一定的SQL语言基础；</p>\n<p>2、针对SQL注入的专项训练推荐使用sqli-labs开源靶场，阅读源码了解后台逻辑有助于进一步理解SQL注入原理；</p>\n<p>3、SQL注入可分为数字型和字符型，不同语句注入的payload不同。</p>\n<p>数字型查询语句为：</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;*&#160;FROM&#160;products&#160;WHERE&#160;category&#160;=&#160;1&#160;--&#160;注入语句为&#160;or&#160;1=1&#160;--</pre>\n<p>字符型查询语句为：</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;*&#160;FROM&#160;products&#160;WHERE&#160;category&#160;=&#160;&#39;value&#39;&#160;--&#160;注入语句为&#160;&#39;or&#160;1=1&#160;--</pre>\n<p>本节实验均基于字符型注入。</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">实验一：检索隐藏数据</span></p>\n<p>首先来看这样一个URL：</p>\n<p>https://insecure-website.com/products?category=Gifts</p>\n<p>是不是非常熟悉，category为查询参数，后台执行的SQL语句为：</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;*&#160;FROM&#160;products&#160;WHERE&#160;category&#160;=&#160;&#39;Gifts&#39;&#160;AND&#160;released&#160;=&#160;1</pre>\n<p>当我们把查询参数变更为Gifts&#39;这样，则查询语句变为了：</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;*&#160;FROM&#160;products&#160;WHERE&#160;category&#160;=&#160;&#39;Gifts&#39;--&#39;&#160;AND&#160;released&#160;=&#160;1</pre>\n<p>原先查询的另一条件released=1就被注释掉了，因此查询会返回所有category = &#39;Gifts&#39;的数据。</p>\n<p>我们进一步将查询参数变更为category=Gifts&#39;+OR+1=1，查询语句变为了：</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;*&#160;FROM&#160;products&#160;WHERE&#160;category&#160;=&#160;&#39;Gifts&#39;&#160;OR&#160;1=1--&#39;&#160;AND&#160;released&#160;=&#160;1</pre>\n<p>结果将会返回products数据表中的所有数据，以此就可进行一次成功的SQL注入。</p>\n<p>在这里再介绍一下不同数据库注释语句的差异（可以发现比较好的通用注释方式即为-- ）</p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p>Oracle：REM 单行注释 -- 单行注释 /*多行注释*/</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p>MS SQL Server： -- 单行注释 /*多行注释*/</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p>MySQL：# 单行注释 -- 单行注释（特别注意，-- 后需跟空格或控制字符） /*多行注释*/</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p>PostgreSQL： -- 单行注释 /*多行注释*/</p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p>这就是这个实验的SQL注入漏洞原理，下面我们进入到实验环境当中：</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image409.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image409-1024x557.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image409-1024x557.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>通过实验介绍，我们知道完成该实验需要执行一次SQL注入以显示所有产品细节，无论是否满足release=1参数。</p>\n<p>为了方便这一系列注入实验的进行，推荐可以安装一个chrome插件Harkbar，注意使用插件后虽然方便直接操作请求，但是需要注意url编码问题，比如 -- 这一注释后的空格是否成功附着到url中，可通过观察地址栏是否为 -- %27进行探查，由于插件本身问题可能存在错误，这时还是推荐使用burpsuite来对请求进行修改。</p>\n<p>这一插件具有许多有用的功能，在chrome环境下安装好后按f12后点击Harkbar切换到相应选项卡，点击LOAD加载当前页面url，点击EXECUTE发送请求。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image410.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image410-1024x212.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image410-1024x212.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">构造如图所示url参数（注意 -- 后的空格），发送请求即可完成sql注入攻击。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image411.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image411-1024x99.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image411-1024x99.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>成功返回结果，实验结束</p>\n<p><br/></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">实验二：颠覆应用程序逻辑（任意用户登录）</span></p>\n<p>我们在一些SQL注入教程中经常能看到类似&#39;or 1=1这样的注入语句用于绕过用户登录验证，在这个实验中学习的正是这样的背后逻辑。</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;*&#160;FROM&#160;users&#160;WHERE&#160;username&#160;=&#160;&#39;&#39;or&#160;1&#160;--&#160;&#39;&#160;AND&#160;password&#160;=&#160;&#39;123&#39;</pre>\n<p>这一条非常经典的在登录过程中，应用后台的数据库查询语句，通过语句执行后的返回值是否为真判断数据库中是否有匹配的账户存在。</p>\n<p>因此，我们只需要构造paylaod使该语句执行结果总为真即可实现任意用户登录，常见的payload如&#39; or 1=1 --</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;*&#160;FROM&#160;users&#160;WHERE&#160;username&#160;=&#160;&#39;&#39;or&#160;1&#160;--&#160;&#39;&#160;AND&#160;password&#160;=&#160;&#39;123&#39;</pre>\n<p>进入实验，实验完成要求：以administrator账号身份登录。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image412.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image412-1024x458.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image412-1024x458.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>进入account login页面，账号值构造如图所示，密码输入任意值。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image413.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image413-1024x476.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image413-1024x476.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>成功登录即可完成实验</p>\n<p><br/></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">实验三：从其他数据表中检索数据（联合查询UNION注入）</span></p>\n<p>在进行sql注入攻击时，我们可以通过union语句进行联合查询，获取其他数据表中的数据，这里以Mysql为例，简要介绍下UNION操作符：</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\"><code style=\"font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Courier, monospace;font-size: 1em;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><span class=\"hljs-keyword\">SELECT</span> expression1, expression2, ... expression_n<br/>FROM <span class=\"hljs-keyword\">tables</span><br/>[<span class=\"hljs-keyword\">WHERE</span> conditions]<br/><span class=\"hljs-keyword\">UNION</span> [<span class=\"hljs-keyword\">ALL</span> | <span class=\"hljs-keyword\">DISTINCT</span>]<br/><span class=\"hljs-keyword\">SELECT</span> expression1, expression2, ... expression_n<br/>FROM <span class=\"hljs-keyword\">tables</span><br/>[<span class=\"hljs-keyword\">WHERE</span> conditions];</code></pre>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">expression1, expression2, ... expression_n：</span>要检索的列；</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">tables：</span>要检索的数据表；</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">WHERE conditions：</span>可选， 检索条件；</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">DISTINCT：</span>可选，删除结果集中重复的数据。默认情况下 UNION 操作符已经删除了重复数据，所以 DISTINCT 修饰符对结果没啥影响；</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">ALL：</span>可选，返回所有结果集，包含重复数据。</p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">SELECT&#160;a,&#160;b&#160;FROM&#160;table1&#160;UNION&#160;SELECT&#160;c,&#160;d&#160;FROM&#160;table2;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;--&#160;从table1中检索a，b并从table2中检索c，d</pre>\n<p>注意执行union查询需要满足两个条件：</p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p>各个查询必须返回相同数量的列；</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p>每个列中的数据类型必须在各个查询之间兼容。</p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p>所以我们在进行union注入时需要先确定查询语句中的列数，在这个实验教程中介绍了两种方法。</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">使用Order By子句</span></p>\n<p>order by子句可以用于对查询结果进行排序，通过接收一个列名为参数或一个简单的能识别特定列的数字。</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs yaml\"><code style=\"font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Courier, monospace;font-size: 1em;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39; UNION SELECT NULL--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">UNION</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">SELECT</span> <span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span><span class=\"hljs-string\">,NULL--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">UNION</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">SELECT</span> <span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span><span class=\"hljs-string\">,NULL,NULL--</span></code></pre>\n<p>通过不断递增指向列的数字，直到返回错误以推断出最大列数。</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs lua\"><code style=\"font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Courier, monospace;font-size: 1em;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39; ORDER BY 1--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span> ORDER BY <span class=\"hljs-number\">2</span><span class=\"hljs-comment\">--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-comment\">&#39; ORDER BY 3--</span></code></pre>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">使用Union子句</span></p>\n<p>如前所述，联合查询需要每个返回的列数相同，因此若列数不同便会返回错误，通过不断递增列直到返回正确信息。</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs yaml\"><code style=\"font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Courier, monospace;font-size: 1em;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39; UNION SELECT NULL--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">UNION</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">SELECT</span> <span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span><span class=\"hljs-string\">,NULL--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">UNION</span> <span class=\"hljs-string\">SELECT</span> <span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span><span class=\"hljs-string\">,NULL,NULL--</span></code></pre>\n<p>接下来进入实验</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image414.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image414-1024x562.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image414-1024x562.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>实验需要我们探测出查询语句中列的正确的数量，并执行SQL注入返回包含null数据的附加列。</p>\n<p>使用order by子句进行猜测，使用&#39;order by 3时成功返回结果。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image415.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image415-1024x73.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image415-1024x73.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>使用&#39;order by 4时返回结果错误，可以推断出查询语句中的列数量为3。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image416.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image416-1024x81.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image416-1024x81.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>使用union查询进行注入攻击，完成实验。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image417.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image417-1024x67.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image417-1024x67.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">实验四：通过SQL UNION注入查找有用的数据类型列</span></p>\n<p>比如我们希望寻找一字符串类型的数据列，我们可以先查明正确的列数量，然后通过不断更换union查询子句中字符列的位置来进行确定。</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs objectivec\"><code style=\"font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Courier, monospace;font-size: 1em;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39; UNION SELECT &#39;</span>a<span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;,NULL,NULL,NULL--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span> UNION SELECT <span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span>,<span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;a&#39;</span>,<span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span>,<span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span>--<br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39; UNION SELECT NULL,NULL,&#39;</span>a<span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;,NULL--</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span> UNION SELECT <span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span>,<span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span>,<span class=\"hljs-literal\">NULL</span>,<span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;a&#39;</span>--</code></pre>\n<p>实验完成条件：实验提供了一个随机的字符串，在查询结果中显示该字符串以完成实验。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image418.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image418-1024x573.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image418-1024x573.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>实验生成的随机字符串</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image419.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image419-1024x134.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image419-1024x134.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>首先通过order by子句确定列数为3，执行union查询，不断替换字符串位置直到返回正确结果。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image420.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image420-1024x42.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image420-1024x42.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image421.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image421-1024x65.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image421-1024x65.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p>返回了有效结果</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image422.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image422-1024x223.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image422-1024x223.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p>使用实验给出的字符串进行替换，发送请求完成实验。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image423.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image423-1024x67.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image423-1024x67.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">实验五：通过SQL UNION注入检索感兴趣的数据</span></p>\n<p>这一实验需要我们通过SQL注入获取到users表中所有的username和password数据，由于实验已经告诉我们所需的数据位于该web应用后台数据库中的莫具体表及字段当中，所以可以直接使用语句进行查询。但在我们实际的渗透测试过程中，存在哪些让人感兴趣的数据是需要通过多次SQL注入进行推断的，其具体细节留在后面章节再具体介绍。</p>\n<p>实验完成条件：通过SQL注入获取账号和密码，并以administrator身份登录。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image424.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image424-1024x575.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image424-1024x575.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>首先使用order by子句判断查询列数，数量为2。</p>\n<p>使用union查询，获取账号信息。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image425.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image425-1024x350.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image425-1024x350.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>使用administrator账号登录，完成实验。</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">实验六：通过字符串连接将多个值返回在一个列中</span></p>\n<p>在上一个实验中，我们使用了&#39;union select username,password -- 这一payload，其成功执行的条件为原先的查询列数也为两列，且数据类型均为字符串类型。但在这一次的实验中，通过‘union select &#39;a&#39;,NULL -- 测试可以发现仅第二列为字符串类型，因此我们需要将两个查询参数合并到一列中。</p>\n<p>使用连接字符串将两个查询参数合并在一起，其返回结果构造类似administrator~s3cure。</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs sql\">&#39;&#160;UNION&#160;SELECT&#160;username&#160;||&#160;&#39;~&#39;&#160;||&#160;password&#160;FROM&#160;users--</pre>\n<p>当然不同数据库的字符串连接方式也不同。</p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\">\n<li>\n<p>Oracle: &#39;foo&#39;||&#39;bar&#39;</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p>SQL Server: &#39;foo&#39;+&#39;bar&#39;</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p>Mysql: &#39;foo&#39; &#39;bar&#39;（空格） CONCAT(&#39;foo&#39;,&#39;bar&#39;)</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p>PostgreSQL: &#39;foo&#39;||&#39;bar&#39;</p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p>实验要求：通过SQL注入获取账号和密码，并以administrator身份登录。</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image426.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image426-1024x658.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image426-1024x658.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>判断字符串位置</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image427.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image427-1024x197.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image427-1024x197.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>构造payload获取账号密码</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image428.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" class=\"zoomImg\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-large\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image428-1024x371.png?x-oss-process=style/medium\" title=\"image428-1024x371.png\" alt=\"image.png\"/></a></p>\n<p class=\"pgc-img-caption\" style=\"margin-top: 16px;margin-bottom: 16px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><br/></p>\n<p>使用administrator成功登录，完成实验。</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 700;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\">总结</span></p>\n<p>本节实验介绍了基础的手动SQL注入实验，汇总一下使用到的注入语句与技巧。</p>\n<pre class=\"syl-page-code hljs cs\"><code style=\"font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Courier, monospace;font-size: 1em;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;border: 0px\"><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;or 1=1&#160; &#160;-- 注入点判断（语句永真）</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span>or order <span class=\"hljs-keyword\">by</span> <span class=\"hljs-number\">3</span> -- 判断查询语句列的数量<br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;union select NULL,&#39;</span>a<span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39; -- 判断特定数据类型列的位置</span><br/><span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;</span>union <span class=\"hljs-keyword\">select</span> NULL,username||<span class=\"hljs-string\">&#39;~&#39;</span>||password&#160;&#160;-- 连接字符串以返回单一行</code></pre>\n<p>想要掌握SQL注入光理解原理是不行的，在学习中还是应该多进行实际的动手操作。</p>\n<p>以上是今天要分享的内容，大家看懂了吗？</p>\n<p><br/></p>\n","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Thu, 27 Aug 2020 06:25:23 0px 3px, rgb(195, 217, 223) 0px 2px, rgb(195, 217, 223) 0px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>什么是序列化和反序列化</strong></section>\n</section>\n</section>\n</section>\n</section>\n<h2 cid=\"n2\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.75em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"></span></h2>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">序列化：将对象转换成一个字符串，PHP序列化函数是:<code style=\"box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;vertical-align: initial;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(231, 234, 237);background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244);border-radius: 3px;padding-right: 2px;padding-left: 2px;font-size: 0.9em;font-family: var(--monospace);\">serialize()</code></span> </p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">反序列化：将序列化后的字符串还原为一个对象，PHP反序列化函数是:<code style=\"box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;vertical-align: initial;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(231, 234, 237);background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244);border-radius: 3px;padding-right: 2px;padding-left: 2px;font-size: 0.9em;font-family: var(--monospace);\">unserialize()</code></span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">在说反序列化漏洞之前我们先了解一下对象概念：</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们举个例子，如果把生物当成一个大类，那么就可以分为动物和植物两个类，而动物又可以分为食草动物和杂食动物，那有人可能会问了，为什么这么分呢？</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">因为动物都有嘴，需要吃东西，植物都需要土空气和水，都会吸取养分，那么这些分类我们可以看成php中的类，动物的嘴和植物需要的土空气水都可以当作属性，动物吃东西和植物吸取养分都可以当作方法。世间的万物我们都可以看成是对象，因为他们都有各自的属性。比如：人有身高，体重，年龄，性别等等这些属性，也可以唱歌，跳舞，跑步等等行为。如果把人看成一个类的话，那么身高，体重，年龄，性别这些就是人这个类的属性，而唱歌，跳舞，跑步就是人这个类的行为。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们来创建一个人类看看，首先要考虑到这个人的姓名(<code style=\"box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;vertical-align: initial;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(231, 234, 237);background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244);border-radius: 3px;padding-right: 2px;padding-left: 2px;font-size: 0.9em;font-family: var(--monospace);\">zhangsan</code>)，性别(<code style=\"box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;vertical-align: initial;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(231, 234, 237);background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244);border-radius: 3px;padding-right: 2px;padding-left: 2px;font-size: 0.9em;font-family: var(--monospace);\">男</code>)，年龄(<code style=\"box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;vertical-align: initial;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(231, 234, 237);background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244);border-radius: 3px;padding-right: 2px;padding-left: 2px;font-size: 0.9em;font-family: var(--monospace);\">50</code>)，还有它会的技能(<code style=\"box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;vertical-align: initial;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(231, 234, 237);background-color: rgb(243, 244, 244);border-radius: 3px;padding-right: 2px;padding-left: 2px;font-size: 0.9em;font-family: var(--monospace);\">会忽悠</code>)。</span></p>\n<section class=\"code-snippet__fix code-snippet__js\">\n<pre data-lang=\"xml\" style=\"margin-top: 0px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 1em 1em 1em style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">看看运行结果:</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: SimSun;\">这就是一个简单的对象了，那我们就将它序列化和反序列化一下。</span></p>\n<section class=\"code-snippet__fix code-snippet__js\">\n<pre class=\"code-snippet__js\">$belles&#160;=&#160;&#160;new&#160;zhangsan();\necho&#160;serialize($belles);\necho&#160;&#34;\\n\\r&#34;;\nunserialize(&#39;O:8:&#34;zhangsan&#34;:2:{s:3:&#34;sex&#34;;s:3:&#34;男&#34;;s:3:&#34;age&#34;;s:2:&#34;50&#34;;}&#39;);\n//&#160;看看它的年龄\necho&#160;$belles-&#62;age;</pre>\n</section>\n<p 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们可以看到实例化就是把对象转换成字符串，反序列化就是把字符串在变成对象，之后就可以使用对象的功能了。</span><br/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">再来看看与PHP反序列化漏洞有关的魔法函数，这些函数不用创建，默认存在的。</span></p>\n<section class=\"code-snippet__fix code-snippet__js\">\n<pre class=\"code-snippet__js\">__destruct()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//对象被销毁时触发\n__construct()&#160;&#160;&#160;//当一个对象创建时被调用\n__wakeup()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//使用unserialize时触发\n__sleep()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//使用serialize时触发\n__toString()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//把类当作字符串使用时触发\n__get()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//获取不存在的类属性时触发\n__set()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//设置不存在的类属性会触发\n__isset()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//在不可访问的属性上调用isset()或empty()触发\n__unset()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//在不可访问的属性上使用unset()时触发\n__invoke()&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;//当脚本尝试将对象调用为函数时触发</pre>\n</section>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">随着云计算的普及的普及，越来越多的企业上云，企业环境和资产形态已由传统的实体化向虚拟化和多样化转换，云计算的灵活性、可扩展性和性价比吸引了更多的企业上云，同时也带来了<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-weight: style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">安全行业的小伙伴应该都明白一个道理，那就是没有绝对安全的系统。而当系统被入侵和破坏时，不可避免的会导致业务中断。应急响应的核心价值就是在安全事件突发时，快速有序的处理，最大限度的快速恢复业务和减少损失。因此响应和恢复速度将是云上应急响应的核心竞争力。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 562px;height: 317px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-1598607380.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">以上是我总结的云上应急响应的现状，从图中可以看到云租户的诉求和运营商的交付方案存在很大的不对等，这也是云上应急的主要矛盾。大量的差评工单和投诉都是因为这个产生的。这也是客户和运营商面临的一个重大难题。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 562px;height: 317px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-15986073801.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"/>既然是难题，难在哪里？从图中我们可以看到有六大困难，并get到三个关键点：<strong>海量事件的困扰，分析投入大、人员要求高；证据完整性的挑战，证据提取和保全难度大；责任共担模型便捷模糊导致权责不清晰。</strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 563px;height: 315px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-1598607381.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">如何解决以上提到的困难？通过上图我们可以看到云平台的主要解决方案是通过云平台基础设施和自动化运维体系构成。通过SOC中集成的云产品日志和全网蜜罐数据进行智能化分析解决云主机自身无日志或日志丢失问题、通过镜像、快照和自动化工具突破网络复杂、应用场景复杂、责任边界模糊、取证苦难和数据量大的困难。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;font-size: 20px;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-weight: bold;\">云时代的原生自动化应急响应</strong></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 563px;height: 317px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-1598607382.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">业内通常使用的PDCERF方法学（最早由 1987 年美国宾夕法尼亚匹兹堡软件工程研究所在关于应急响应的邀请工作会议上提出），将应急响应分成准备（Preparation）、检测（Detection）、抑制（Containment）、根除（Eradication）、恢复（Recovery）、跟踪（Follow-up）6个阶段的工作。从上图可以看到一次完整的应急响应需要做的事情很多。而业内的提到应急响应一般仅进行到第二个阶段，比较好的运营商会进行到第四个阶段。无论第二还是第四阶段都是建立在解决问题的角度，无法进行持续性运营和方案进化。常规的应急响应对人力和能力的要求很高。且无法解决上边提到的六个难点问题。为了更好的在云上做好应急响应。腾讯安全云鼎实验室结合多年的云上运营和实践经验设计出云原生自动化应急方案。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 563px;height: 315px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-1598607383.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\"><strong>此方案遵守三大原则：</strong></span></section>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\" style=\"margin: 0px 8px 16px;padding: 0px 0px 0px 2em;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\">\n<li>\n<section style=\"line-height: 2em;margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\"><strong>•&#160;整个系统运行环境和资源均在用户vpc内</strong></span></section>\n</li>\n<li>\n<section style=\"line-height: 2em;margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\"><strong>•&#160;操作由用户账号发起/用户授权</strong></span></section>\n</li>\n<li>\n<section style=\"line-height: 2em;margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\"><strong>•&#160;所有证据数据和分析结果均保留于用户vpc空间</strong></span></section>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">整个方案分为两大部分：被动响应和主动发现。本方案采用CS架构，结合云平台多年运营经验、SOC、全网蜜罐和威胁情报的数据进行自动化智能分析。从而帮助应急响应人员在最短时间内定位入侵途径、完成电子取证和输出应急策略。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">被动溯源分为三个阶段：</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\"></span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">第一阶段：</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">当客户发生入侵事件后，通过自助授权后会启动溯源主机中的谛听系统。谛听系统会申请镜像授权，当授权通过后，会创建临时API KEY并根据要求进行快照或镜像。当镜像打包完毕会进行镜像挂载或者加载快照进行常规溯源。常规溯源会覆盖九大检测场景。如果溯源结束会输出报告和证据；</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">第二阶段：</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">如果溯源失败。会自动拉取SOC的行为检测数据、全网蜜罐的入侵还原数据以及威胁情报的IOCS数据进行智能化数据分析。分析后会输出报告和证据；</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">第三阶段：</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">如果溯源结束，将会输出相关IOCS到log中，输出未知检测告警，通过人工进行最终溯源。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">主动溯源由SOC、蜜罐、威胁情报构成：SOC的行为检测数据会实时输出异常告警，并提供告警溯源；全网蜜罐进行入侵数据采集，还原数据入侵路径，并输出IOCS进行特征匹配，输出溯源结果和报告；根据威胁情报的IOCS数据进行特征匹配，输出溯源结果和报告。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">接下来我们通过被动关系和主动关系构建来看看整个数据是如何关联和分析的。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 562px;height: 314px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-1598607384.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">上图展示了整个溯源方案的被动关系构建图谱:通过入侵时间将恶意命令、服务、登录日志、服务日志、进程网络等数据关联起来，并通过算法、逻辑和入侵特征判定入侵途径。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 563px;height: 316px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-15986073841.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">主动关系的构建通过SOC和蜜罐数据来完成：SOC流量日志和进程日志通过域名或者IP等进行关联；服务指纹和文件/木马特征通过基线和木马行为进行特征关联；SOC和蜜罐数据通过聚类校验和回归验证判断入侵行为。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><img style=\"border: 0px;width: 562px;height: 317px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139910-1598607385.jpeg\"/><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">￼</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;word-spacing: 0px;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 2;widows: 2;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: normal;\">对于被动检测和主动检测无法覆盖的未知入侵方式、文件和行为将会以日志的方式打印出来。通过查看日志可以得知云安全产品和溯源工具的检测能力等。从而针对性的进行改进，持续进化自身，驱动和完善云安全产品。</span></section>\n<section style=\"margin: 15px 8px;color: rgb(51, 51, 51);text-transform: none;line-height: 2em;text-indent: 0px;letter-spacing: normal;font-family: &#34;Helvetica Neue&#34;,Helvetica,&#34;Segoe UI&#34;,Arial,freesans,sans-serif;font-size: 16px;font-style: rgb(234, 249, 253);text-shadow: rgb(1, 115, 99) 1px 1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) 1px -1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) 1px -1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) -1px 1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) -1px -1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) 0px 1.4px, rgb(1, 115, 2px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>0x02 查看各种记录</strong></section>\n</section>\n</section>\n</section>\n</section>\n<h1 cid=\"n10\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"></span></h1>\n<h2 cid=\"n12\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.75em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;color: #1C7892;\">更新日志</span></h2>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我在 GITHUB上找到了一个合适的开源 CMS项目。在其官网上可以看到该CMS的更新的日志。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">查看更新日志（CHANGELOG）：</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583668.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们可以看到 1.2.3 版本修复了一个 SQL 盲注 (Issue#19) 和 1.2.4版本修复了一个文件管理器上传漏洞 (Issue#20)。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">查看该 CMS 的代码结构，发现是基于 CodeIgniter 框架(后文简称 CI )进行的二次开发。对 CI 的相关类进行了继承，并自己封装了函数，进行一些特殊处理。</span></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n19\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.75em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;color: #1C7892;\">ISSUE记录</span></h2>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们先来看下这个 SQL 盲注，首先访问下 GITHUB 上 Issue#19 的页面看下详情。</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583670.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583672.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">这个是一个 1.2.2版本上报的 ISSUE 信息，从中我们可以看出这位漏洞上报者来自 ABT 实验室。漏洞信息非常全面，格式优美，图文并茂。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">在 Issue 中不但给出了问题文件的路径是/core/MY_Security.php ，还给出了 Payload 细节：在前端登录时，User-Agent: &#39;-( if( condition, sleep(5), 1))-&#39;&#39;, &#39;192.168.1.11&#39;,&#39;time&#39;)# 。并且将漏洞产生原因进行了详细阐述：由于参数缺失，该 CMS 会记录下该登录包的信息，以&#34;无效的 CSRF 防护&#34;为原因写入数据库。但是信息中的 HTTP_USER_AGENT 这个参数未作任何检测，就直接拼接到 SQ L语句中，故造成了漏洞可以被利用。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">在最后漏洞上报者还给出了修复建议。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们根据给出了文件名找到了 1.2.2 版本的 MY_Securtiy.php 文件。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">MY_Securtiy 是继承 CI 框架的 CI_Security，并对其一些常用函数进行了封装扩展。</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583676.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们的目标函数 csrf_show_error就是其中之一，我们先来看下该函数的调用过程：</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583679.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">调用在CI框架中的 Security.php 文件：在 csrf 验证时，如果 csrf_token 不合法，则会调用csrf_show_error 函数。所以我们在构建请求报文时，需要将 csrf_token 参数不设置或者改动一下。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">CI_Security中的csrf_show_error:只有错误显示。</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583686.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">My_Security中的csrf_show_error:增加了对错误登录的记录入库并细分了错误种类。</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583688.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">第45行，即漏洞上报者提到的condition，如果语句不会被执行，则count也不会增加，所以条件一直为true。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">第46行，可以看出直接将 $_SERVER[&#39;HTTP_USER_AGENT&#39;] 拼接到 SQL 的 INSERT 语句中，并没有任何过滤，所以产生了SQL 注入。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">看起来简单明了，这个漏洞应该会被完美的修复掉。但事实上这个漏洞修复的过程并没有这么简单。在这个Issue#19中后续有一段很有趣的CMS开发者和漏洞上报者之间的对话记录，引起了我的兴趣：</span></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n40\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.75em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;color: #1C7892;\">聊天记录</span></h2>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583694.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">漏洞上报的版本为 1.2.2，而这时开发者已经开发出了 1.2.3-rev1版本，并且尝试修复这个 SQL 注入的问题，并希望漏洞上报者使用 1.2.3-rev1 来看看是否修复了此漏洞。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">这个漏洞上报者非常有耐心，他在实际尝试后发现问题并没有被修复的同时，还查看1.2.3-rev1 的 MY_Security.php 的代码。他告诉CMS开发者使用 xss_clean 函数并不能解决 SQL注入的问题，并且告诉他应该使用正确的函数为：escape-string 或者real_escape_string 这两个函数来防止 SQL 注入，并给出了这两个函数在PHP.NET 的官方链接和以及修复之后的代码以及测试结果。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">再来看之后的对话：</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583699.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">这个CMS开发者很勤奋，第二天就放出了 1.2.3-rev2 版本尝试修复了这个问题，并且再次邀请漏洞上报者测试是否修复此问题。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">漏洞上报者于当日确认已经修复，Payload 不再起作用，然后开发者关闭了此问题。至此一个开源 CMS 的安全问题被修复了。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"><br/></span></p>\n<h1 cid=\"n49\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 2.25em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"></span></h1>\n<section>\n<section style=\"text-align: left;margin: 10px auto;\">\n<section style=\"display: style=\"text-align: center;letter-spacing: 3px;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(234, 249, 253);text-shadow: rgb(1, 115, 99) 1px 1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) 1px -1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) 1px -1px, rgb(1, 115, 99) -1px mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 2.25em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"></span></h1>\n<h2 cid=\"n51\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.75em;margin: 1rem 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们这个开发者是有基本安全意识的，该 CMS 包含 xxs_clean 函数，证明开发者在已经意识到 XSS 问题并且封装了相应的函数来做过滤处理。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">但是该开发者对于安全问题的细节认识并不太清晰。在碰到 SQL 注入问题时企图用 xss_clean 来解决这个问题，这点说明他对于 SQL 注入产生的原因和修复方法并不太明确。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们来看下GITHUB上 1.2.3-rev2 版本中开发者对于这个问题的修复方案：</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583704.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">开发者很听话，使用了 escape_string 来修复 SQL 注入的问题，做的很好。但是他并没有去掉 xss_clean 方法，而是在escape_string 调用之后仍然还继续调用xss_clean 方法。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">这是为什么呢？我们来尝试猜测开发者的想法：在1.2.3-rev2版本中使用xss_clean后未修复，于是加上了escape_string来修复该漏洞。xss_clean 是处理危险字符的方法，escape_string也是处理危险字符的方法，两个过滤危险字符的方法叠加起来，理应是更安全的。就像两个 WAF 串联叠加，不应该是难上加难吗？</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">但是事实可能并非如此，也许正是这种情况给了我们绕过机会！</span></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n61\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.75em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;color: #1C7892;\">绕过修复方案</span></h2>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">首先看一下 escape_string 到底转义了哪些字符:</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">下列字符受影响：</span></p>\n<ul class=\" list-paddingleft-2\" cid=\"n64\" mdtype=\"list\" style=\"padding-left: 30px;font-size: 16px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\">\n<li>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">x00</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">n</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">r</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\"></span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">&#39;</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">&#34;</span></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin-right: 5px;margin-bottom: 0.5rem;margin-left: 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">x1a</span></p>\n</li>\n</ul>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">由于这段 SQL 注入是字符型，我们需要 &#39; 来闭合语句，但是 escape_string 会将 &#39; 变为 &#39; 从而阻止 SQL 注入。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们来看下 xss_clean 中的代码：</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583706.png\"/></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">第 354-365 行是一个递归调用。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">第 368行是一个移除不可见字符的方法，如：x00、x01 等等。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">第 379-389 行是我们的关键代码，这段代码是判断 $str 参数中是否包含 % 字符，如果有的话就判定为需要 URL 解码并且调用 rawurldecode 来进行 URL 解码。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">这个不就是我们要找的代码吗？！</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">escape_string 方法并不会转义 % ，所以我们将 Payload 进行 URL 编码后并不会被 escape_string 方法改变任何内容。而当到达 xss_clean 时 Payload 将被 URL 解码，从而绕过了对 SQL 注入的过滤。</span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" src=\"https://secpulseoss.oss-cn-shanghai.aliyuncs.com/wp-content/uploads/1970/01/beepress-image-139876-1598583710.jpeg\"/></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><br/></p>\n<h2 cid=\"n89\" mdtype=\"heading\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;break-after: avoid-page;break-inside: avoid;font-size: 1.75em;margin: 1rem 5px;font-weight: bold;cursor: text;padding-bottom: 0.3em;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238);white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;color: #1C7892;\">漏洞验证</span></h2>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">我们先来测试下原来的 Payload：</span></p>\n<section class=\"code-snippet__fix code-snippet__js\">\n<pre class=\"code-snippet__js\">**&#39;-(&#160;if((1=1),&#160;sleep(5),&#160;1)&#160;)-&#39;&#39;,&#160;&#39;192.168.1.11&#39;,&#39;time&#39;)&#160;#**</pre>\n</section>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">没有造成延时，原 Payload 失败。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 2.5px;font-family: Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;\"><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;color: #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">新的 Payload 就是将原 Payload 进行 URL 编码，新 Payload：</span></p>\n<section class=\"code-snippet__fix code-snippet__js\">\n<pre class=\"code-snippet__js\">**%27%2d%28%20%69%66%28%28%31%3d%31%29%2c%20%73%6c%65%65%70%28%35%29%2c%20%31%29%20%29%2d%27%27%2c%20%27%31%39%32%2e%31%36%38%2e%31%2e%31%31%27%2c%27%74%69%6d%65%27%29%20%23**</pre>\n</section>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" style=\"width: 100%;height: auto;\" #585858;font-family: 宋体, SimSun;\">造成延时成功，绕过修复方案，触发 SQL 时间盲注漏洞。</span></p>\n<p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;orphans: 4;margin: 0.8em 5px;white-space: pre-wrap;font-size: 16px;line-height:
